< text>
‚Äî96% Increase On Rent After 5 Months!!!‚Äî

I rarely write negative reviews, but I am shocked by the corporate greed and predatory pricing practices of Extra Space Storage.

After an unexpected death in the family, we ended up needing to rent 2 units from Extra Space on short notice.  A few months later, Extra Space increased the monthly cost of both units, nearly DOUBLING the cost of one unit.  The process of figuring out what happened has revealed Extra Space's profit-at-all-costs business model, and a stunning lack of transparency.

Understandably surprised and shocked at a 96% increase, I spoke to the call center, district manager, and building manager to see if this was a mistake.  Each understood our frustration, but informed me that the "market rate" for that unit was now almost double.  The district manager explained that the rate changes all the time based on computer algorithms.

To verify this, we did quite a bit of research online and found that we could still get the exact size unit in the SAME FACILITY for $130‚Äîone dollar less than we initially rented it for.  Moreover similar units were available in the area from competitors in the same price range, so it seems Extra Space's algorithm and market rate excuse did not hold water.

When we called asked them to match THEIR OWN PRICE, they said that we were not eligible couldn‚Äôt get that deal because we were not ‚Äúfirst time renters.‚Äù  Reviewing our original paperwork when we originally signed up, it is clear that we were never given any sort of promotion, and nowhere in the fine print did it mention that we were being offered a rate for being for first time renters.  In fact, our rate was simply described as the ‚Äúweb rate‚Äù or ‚Äúflash sale" and listed no qualifications or exclusions.  Extra Space had created this loophole to benefit themselves after the fact.

The Extra Space corporate call center had a district team lead named Paul reach out to us regarding this.  Unfortunately, instead of de-escalating the situation, he could not properly explain the inconsistencies in my rent increase.   Furthermore, he could not provide me with any statement on their website that referenced the restrictions they were mentioning verbally.  Paul informed me that he would ‚Äúallow" me to have that web rate, but‚Äîastoundingly‚Äîlater retracted the rate even though I had a CONFIRMATION EMAIL that guaranteed the rate in writing.

This extraordinary runaround from Extra Space and their employees in a period of incredible grief for our family has been nothing short of astounding, compassionless, and time-wasting.

I spoke with a rep at A-1 Storage and they only raise the rent for tenants 10% a year.  If nothing else, we‚Äôd like other renters to be warned about Extra Space Storage and their secretive predatory rent increase practices.</text>

< text>
Came into the Burberry store since they had a really great sale online and the scarves I wanted were only sold in store. When we got here, however, we were disappointed that all of their sale items were gone. They said it was ‚Äúdue to their relocation‚Äù so all of the  sale items were sold first. I guess that‚Äôs understandable.

With their scarves, it‚Äôs so important to look at them in store. There‚Äôs only so much you can tell from online, such as the fit, the feel of the fabric, and how it looks on you. Because they didn‚Äôt have custom embroidery available in the store, I only came in just to browse which one would be better to purchase but I did end up buying the classic cashmere scarf online so I could get the tan embroidery for free.

If you have a shop runner account, you get free 2-day shipping. Since the delivery time was equivalent for home or in-store delivery, I opted for in-store so I could also pick up the shopping bag (they‚Äôll only do gift wrapping if you ship to your home.) The personalization definitely takes more time to prepare but I kid you not, once the work was completed and the item had been marked as shipped, I received it 24 hours later. Talk about speed!

Picking it up at the store was a breeze. Just had to show them my email confirmation with my order number and despite the email requiring you to show your photo ID and the card you used to purchase it, I did not need to show it to them.

The only reason why I docked them a star was because I had ordered my mom‚Äôs scarf the day before I decided to order one for myself and for some reason I received mine two days before hers. I emailed customer service and they said that some orders take longer than others but it was literally the same scarf with the same colored embroidery and the letters ‚ÄúAZC‚Äù seem harder to have embroidered than ‚ÄúCRZ‚Äù so I‚Äôm not sure what happened there.

I also was a bit disappointed in the package display. Yes, they‚Äôll wrap your product in gift wrapping if you opt for it, which in this case is wrapping the item with tissue paper and sealing with the Burberry signature sticker inside a sturdy cardboard box, which is then placed inside their bag. I didn‚Äôt like that the bags looked as if they had been through some work, as in there were some scuffs and dents that seemed like they traveled some ways to get to me.

I also thought it was odd how my own scarf did not have ribbon tied around the box and the bag but my mom‚Äôs did. It almost gives me the impression that it just depends on who‚Äôs working at that time that will determine to what level of presentation their team wants to put forward. To me, that‚Äôs not a good look but I guess I‚Äôm just nitpicking.

Overall, I did enjoy my shopping experience here and plan to purchase more products in the future. I do hope that they take my suggestions quite seriously regarding the packaging and presentation. They‚Äôre still a designer store in my books, so I would hope that they‚Äôd like to continue providing the same level of excellence that their competitors consistently provide.<//text>

< Review>
My wife and I were there during our vacation over the Christmas holiday when she spotted a $5,000 leather Burberry coat that was on sale that she wanted. They didn't have her small size until a girl named Erica found one in the back. We carefully inspected it right there and then, and it was flawless, so I decided that I was going to get it as a Christmas present for my wife. I wanted it shipped back to my home state, and I had asked for a Burberry box since it was a gift. When we came back from our vacation on Christmas day, the Burberry coat had arrived. Not only did it NOT come with a gift box, but it also had this quarter-size pen mark on the collar, and someone had tried to clean it off, but left a bigger mark there instead. The coat was placed backwards inside a garment bag, so that we couldn't see the pen mark and damage when we first unzipped the bag. I had never seen my wife so disappointed and shocked before when we took the coat out. This was deliberately done. We both grew up in Southern California, went to UCLA and then UCSF for medical school. We shopped at South Coast Plaza all of our lives. This is South Coast Plaza, and there is a standard here, a high one, that keeps us and many others coming back again and again. Whether this Erica girl deliberately sent us a marked and damaged $5,000 leather Burberry coat or not I can't be sure. But what I am certain of, is that she was in charge of the handling of that coat, and to get it to us (it was NOT damaged when we were there inspecting it).  And that is how it arrived to us damaged. Whether it is her or someone in shipping or anyone else there who handled this coat after we purchased it, this should have never happened, and the damaged coat should never have been sent out or sold to a customer. You would think the Burberry employees at South Coast Plaza were trained better than this. We thought we were going to have one of the best Christmas in a long time, but instead it became one of the worst ever. We will never shop at Burberry at South Coast Plaza again. I would rather take my business to the Rodeo Drive or the San Diego locations, since their customer service are head and shoulders above, and I know that my expensive purchases will be handled correctly, as they always have been before, and that we will never be disappointed.  I will post a picture of the damage that they did to the coat after we had purchased it as soon as I figure out how to on Yelp!< /Review>

<review>What began as my cheapest solution to my cracked screen problem became an expensive one.

On September 14, 2017, I spoke with Justin and entrusted merchant, Cheapest IPhone Repair (CIR) to have my cracked glass screen on my phone (Samsung Galaxy S7 Edge) to be repaired. They gave me an estimated finished date of 5 days, but they took almost 2 weeks. Their excuse was that the phone was shipped back "incomplete" aka, they cracked my screen while shipping it.
On September 28, 2017, I was notified via phone that my cell phone was repaired and ready to be picked up. I went the same day to pick up my phone and noticed that it was not in the condition that it was given. To elaborate, CIR was able to repair the screen, but damaged my center home button of the phone when returned to me. After noticing this damage, I spoke with Carlos from CIR that the home button was not how it was given and the button was very loose (think "see-saw" action). Carlos expressed that he noticed the difference and he would speak to his boss. I left that day without my phone for CIR to resolve this issue.
On September 30, 2017, I was contacted by Carlos about the issue. Carlos stated that he spoke with his boss and said that CIR can try to fix the home button, which they couldn‚Äôt guarantee. CIR also stated that I would have to pay for the screen if it was broken during the repair process, which was quoted at $220. When asked if there were any other options, Carlos from CIR said, ‚ÄúThis is all we can do.‚Äù I came into CIR to have my cracked glass repaired. However, they wanted me to potentially pay for a cracked screen for their own mistake. As a consumer, it makes sense that CIR would pay and/or fix what was their error. As a result of not wanting to potentially pay for a broken screen, I picked up my phone.

The use of the home button is essential for security (fingerprint sensor) and maneuvering phone applications.  Without the proper use and mechanism, it would render the phone useless and not functional. Even though the button is functioning presently, the loose, ‚Äúsee-saw‚Äù action of the button does not give me confidence that it will last, nor did I give the phone to CIR in this condition.

What began as my cheapest solution to my cracked screen problem was becoming an expensive one.

In brief, I came in with a problem and went out with another one.</review>< Rate>

<Rate>5<//Rate><Review>I visited this store to get screens replaced on an iPad 2 and an iPad mini ($190 total price, 30-day guarantee).

The Apple repair service (Out-of-warranty) costs for these items are as follows:
iPad mini: $199
iPad 2: $249
Plus a $6.95 shipping fee. Fees are in USD and exclude local tax.

The store itself can be accessed via the elevator in the corridor between Gen KBBQ and Northern Cafe. There are doors on both sides of the building to get to the elevator.

When arriving to the store I was greeted immediately by Justin, who provided a quick assessment of my devices' conditions and a reasonable pricing for the overall repair.  After dropping the iPads off, I was expecting the job to be completed late in the afternoon or the next day, but I received a phone call only an hour later that the task was completed - Carlos and Justin were able to get the work done quickly after finishing up another repair order.

I returned to the store soon afterward and found both devices in solid condition.  Justin went through the final steps of heat-drying the adhesive and demonstrated the functionality of the new screens and other device functions.

Overall, I am very satisfied with the job and would recommend this store to anyone looking for mobile device repair services.  I also purchased a new, grandma-proof, dual-layer, protective case for an add-on price of $15! <username>Michelle Morgan</username><Date>1576211023739< /Date><rating>5</rating>< Text>
Happened to be working off site today in the neighborhood.   I previously past Kopan Ramen and caught my attention.  Today on my lunch break I made sure to stop in.  I've also been dealing with a horrible cough too so broth was something I definitely needed.

I ordered the red dragon ramen as part of my combo lunch special.  I selected the seafood gyoza as my side.  The red dragon is rated spicy and indeed it is, but in a manageable way, if you like it spicy.  The broth was delicious and very coating for my throat.  The noodles were good.  My ramen came with fatty pork and it was very tender, easily edible with chop sticks.  Definitely recommend stopping if you're in the area.< /Text>

< Name>
Cindy Swain</Name>
<Date>1536943127938</Date><user>105233314546446653285</user>< Review>
The ramen here has a strange film that forms over the top of the broth - maybe some cheap thickening agent? The red miso broth is creamy but not the way miso usually is. Both the black ramen and red miso ramen textures were wrong. The chasu pork was very low quality and my egg was completely hard boiled, not soft. Overall, some of the worst ramen I've had not out of a packet.

The service here is deplorable. The waiter dropped half a tray of water glasses on my friend and did not apologize or comp any of his meal. We had to flag him down several times for more water refills, and the orders were all screwed up when they came out. Definitely go to any other ramen place in Westwood.< /Review>

< Text>
Happy Lemon is a very corporate place for bubble tea and a salted cream cheese mix that they mix into drinks. That doesn't appeal to me, but it's some I've never seen before, which is always cool to come across.

What really did make my mouth water was their fruit teas. I had their strawberry fruit tea with boba. The boba are sweet. There were mashed up bits of strawberry at the bottom, yum!

The drink was good except I asked fo 50% ice which was a mistake. The ice was totally melted by the time the drink was ready, so it was too warm.I think it would have been delicious otherwise.

I really want to try the lemon slushies and the mango boba. They have a wide variety of toppings. There were a couple  whole sections of the menu I was unfamiliar with, but I'm not super experienced with this sort of thing.

The store was loud, hectic, and busy. There was a long line, but it moved quickly. The people behind the counter were working hard; it was just really popular.

I'll definitely go back and try other things.< /Text>

<rate>4</rate><date>1436492203846</date><Gmap_id>0x80c2b8e720651abb:0x9beff37addede928</Gmap_id>< name>
Tony C</name>
<response>None</response>< text>
Chose these guys for a residential window tint and film in the bathroom based solely off online reviews.  Initially was impressed with the response and follow up that led to the meeting for a price quote.   Estimate seemed a bit high at first but figured it was worth it with all the good reviews to get the job done right.

The installers arrived as scheduled and called before knocking on the door which I appreciated.  So the install begins for the tint on a bay window and some privacy film on a bathroom window.  I work on the laptop in another room while the installers do their thing and give them their space.  2 hours later I get the tap on the shoulder they're done, so I give it a look and from a distance everything looks good,  So I write the check and they're on their way.  I go to inspect closer and notice that the wood floors under the bay window they did was soaked with the over spray and droppings of the liquid they used to apply the window tint.  It's a mess my wife ends up having to take a half hour to clean with the Swifter.

I go up to the bathroom to inspect the film install and see that the toilet under the window they worked on has been displaced about an inch.  So I have to have the toilet re-seated with a new wax ring to make sure there's no leaks.  All in all, you may think, not a big deal but it was a huge disappointment to me.  Such a simple thing to clean up after yourself or lay a cover down at the get go so there's nothing to clean up in the first place.  And if you move a toilet like that, let the owner know and deal with it instead of acting like nothing happened and bailing on it.

7/9/15- Update
Today I received a call from David, one of the owners, inquiring about this issue. I was impressed with his concern over the problem and going to the length he did to make it right.  He was passionate about his service being great and assured me this was to be addressed with his installers.  I wasn't big on ever using them again but the fact they addressed the problem and in the manner they did I would definitely consider them again. If there's a problem and no solution, I'm done with them. I'm in the service industry and understand there will be issues but to me it's not so much the issue, rather how it's handled.  David stepped up and dealt with this head on and I not only respect that but admire it. These guys truly stand behind their work, no matter what that takes.  Originally a 2 star review changed to 4.< /text>

I have been to  this restaurant about 5 times, mostly a  popular place for company get togethers. The venue is excellent for large gatherings. Yes they have a bars with variety drink selections. So if you  want a nice place with  food that everyone can enjoy, Mediterranean style with a bit of Persian influence then this is a place to come. They also have pizza which is average when it comes to flavor.  No wow factor in the pizza. The ingredients are good and fresh.  The service is good.  The food in terms of flavoring and execution is average. I have had much better kebabs in many other Persian or Afghani restaurants  throughout the bay area. The marination is simpler and blander in flavor than other places I have been to. But, the quality of the ingredients is good. They have good starters and finger food for those who want to just have something light and drinks in a group.The menu is balanced and does have some good selections for everyone to try. Do I crave to go to this restaurant for the food ever?  Never but if  I had no where else to go ,  yes I would come here to eat as a viable option. My rating for this place is 3.5 but I will  round  it to 4 just for ambience and quality of ingredients plus I cannot give a 3.5 :) rating on google review.</text>

<rating>4<//rating>< text>
Stopped here for lunch on our way to Carmel. What a great find. Staff was very welcoming and we were seated right away. They brought out pita bread and cucumber salad then an additional tray of hummus, baba  ganoush and tzatiki. Everything was delicious so far!

We ordered a chicken sandwich and a chicken kabob for lunch.

The chicken kabob came with saffron rice and broccoli. Yum. Everything cooked well and chicken was tender and juicy.

Sandwich had avocado, lettuce, tomato and onion with an aioli served on a toasted soft roll. Delicious.

We were glad we made the detour here to have lunch. Yum!</text>

<Name>Suvadeep Banerjee</Name>< Date>
1584246442639<//Date>
<rate>4< /rate>< Review>
I and my wife have long wanted to go to this place, since we live in the apartment right above the restaurant! And finally one night we decided to turn up here. This is quite a unique restaurant in the sense that it caters multiple cuisines - Italian, Persian, American and others.

We decided to try out the chef's soup of the day - a seafood gumbo soup which turned out to be absolutely delicious. As appetizers, we tried out the combo kabab from the usual dinner menu and a kashk-e bademjan based dish from a special menu. The combo kabab had one beef kabab and a chicken kabab which were absolutely delectable, succulent and mouth-watering. One particular aspect that I noticed is that the portion sizes of the kabob plates are smaller than ones in other Persian restaurants in the vicinity (read DishDash, Chellokababi and similar ones). The special entree was a little off-key to our taste.

The service was really great, we enjoyed our time here and the interior is quite classy. I plan to be back here to try the pizzas.</Review>
